    SELECT m."Id", m."CategoryId", m."CreatedAt", m."Description", m."ImageUrl", m."IsAvailable", m."IsDeleted", m."IsManuallyDisabled", m."Name", m."PreparationTime", m."Price", m."UpdatedAt"
    FROM "MenuItems" AS m
    WHERE NOT (m."IsDeleted")
    ORDER BY m."Name"
    LIMIT @p1 OFFSET @p
) AS m0
INNER JOIN "Categories" AS c ON m0."CategoryId" = c."Id"
ORDER BY m0."Name"
